        <header>
    <h2 class="node-title"><a href="/articles/20150817/547/working-riot" title="Working at Riot">Working at Riot</a></h2>
  </header>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Working at Riot" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>

<script type="text/javascript">
    google.load('visualization', '1.1', {packages: ['corechart', 'controls'],'language': 'pt-br'});
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
   
          function montaDataParaGraficoMercadoFuturo(papel){
            drawVisualization(papel);
        }

        function drawVisualization(papel) {
            historicos = [];

            historicos = papel.historicos;

            data_final_cortada = historicos[historicos.length - 1].data.split("/");

            var indice_data_corte = 4

            if ( historicos.length  < indice_data_corte)
                data_inicial_cortada = historicos[historicos.length - 1].data.split("/");
            else
                data_inicial_cortada = historicos[historicos.length - indice_data_corte].data.split("/");

            var dashboard = new google.visualization.Dashboard(document.getElementById('grafico'));

            var control = new google.visualization.ControlWrapper({
             'controlType': 'ChartRangeFilter',
             'containerId': 'control',
             'options': {
               // Filter by the date axis.
               'filterColumnIndex': 0,
               'ui': {
                 'chartType': 'LineChart',
                 'chartOptions': {
                   'chartArea': {'width': '80%'},
                   'hAxis': {'baselineColor': 'none'}
                 },
                 // Display a single series that shows the closing value of the stock.
                 // Thus, this view has two columns: the date (axis) and the stock value (line series).
                 'chartView': {
                   'columns': [0, 1]
                 },
                 // 1 day in milliseconds = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 = 86,400,000
                 'minRangeSize': 86400000
               }
             },
             // Initial range: 2012-02-09 to 2012-03-20.
              'state': {'range': {'start': new Date(data_inicial_cortada[2],(data_inicial_cortada[1]-1),data_inicial_cortada[0]), 
                                 'end': new Date(data_final_cortada[2],(data_final_cortada[1]-1),data_final_cortada[0])}}
           });
        
           var chart = new google.visualization.ChartWrapper({
             'chartType': 'LineChart',
             'containerId': 'chart',
             'options': {
                hAxis: {  
                    baselineColor: '#94bbd1', 
                    gridlines: {color: '#94bbd1'}, 
                    textStyle: {color: '#1f1f1f', fontSize: '10', bold: true},
                },
                vAxis: {  
                    baselineColor: '#3a648c ', 
                    gridlines: {color: '#6594b4'}, 
                    textStyle: {color: '#1f1f1f', fontSize: '10', bold: true},
                },
                backgroundColor: '#94bbd1',
                colors: ['#3a648c'],
                legend: {'position': 'none'},
                pointSize:3,

             },
             // Convert the first column from 'date' to 'string'.
             'view': {
               'columns': [
                 {
                   'calc': function(dataTable, rowIndex) {
                     return dataTable.getFormattedValue(rowIndex, 0);
                   },
                   'type': 'string'
                 }, 1]
             }
           });

           var data = new google.visualization.DataTable();
           data.addColumn('date', 'Date');
           data.addColumn('number', 'Fechamento');

            // var formaxcztter = new Intl.NumberFormat("ru", {
            //   style: "decimal",
            // });

           var len = historicos.length;
            $.each(historicos, function(i){
                data_cortada = historicos[i].data.split("/");
                date = new Date(data_cortada[2],(data_cortada[1]-1),data_cortada[0]);
                data.addRow([date, historicos[i].valor]);
                if (i == len - 1) {
                  $('.pontos-numero').html(_currency(historicos[i].valor, "", 2));
                }
            });

            var formatter = new google.visualization.DateFormat({pattern: "dd/MM"});
            formatter.format(data, 0);

            var formatter = new google.visualization.NumberFormat({
                fractionDigits: 2
                //prefix: 'R$ '
            });
            formatter.format(data, 1);

            dashboard.bind(control, chart);
            dashboard.draw(data);
            $("#grafico").css( "overflow", "hidden" );
            $("#grafico").css( "width", "280px" );
        }

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var d = new Date();
    var strDate = d.getDate() + "/" + (d.getMonth()+1) + "/" + d.getFullYear();

    $('.cambio-data').html(strDate);
    $('.data').html(strDate);
</script>

<script>
    function valida(email) {
        var filtro_mail = /([\w\-]+\@[\w\-]+\.[\w\-]+)/;
        if (!filtro_mail.test(email) || email == "") {
            document.getElementById("newsletter_email").style.border = "1px solid #E32036";
            document.getElementById("newsletter_email").style.color = "#E32036";
            document.getElementById("newsletter_email").setAttribute('placeholder', "Favor preencher um e-mail válido!");
            document.getElementById("newsletter_email").focus();
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    function valida_politica_privacidade(){
        if(!($('#politica_privacidade').is(":checked"))){
            alert('Para inscrever-se a receber newsletters você deve aceitar a nossa  política de privacidade')
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    $('#newsletter_form').submit(function (form) {
        var values = {};
        values['revista'] = '2';
        values['email'] = $('#newsletter_email').val();
        form.preventDefault();
        var valida_email = valida(values['email']);
        if ((valida_email) && (valida_politica_privacidade())){
            $.post('/dinamico/newsletter/', values)
                    .done(function (data) {
                        document.getElementById("newsletter_email").style.border = "1px solid #005b2d";
                        document.getElementById("newsletter_email").style.color = "#005b2d";
                        document.getElementById("newsletter_email").value = '';
                        document.getElementById("newsletter_email").setAttribute('placeholder', "E-mail cadastrado com sucesso!");
                    });
        }
        else {
            return false;
        }
    });
</script>

  function getCookie(name) {
      var value = "; " + document.cookie;
      var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
      if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
  }

  function getCADUNID() {

    var cadunId = getCookie('CADUN_ID');
    cadunId = cadunId.replace(/['"]+/g, '');
    
    return cadunId.substring(0, 10);

  }

  function getCookieGADS() {

    var gads = getCookie('__gads');
    return gads.split(':')[0].split('=')[1];

  }


  var globoId = getCADUNID();
  var iddfp = getCookieGADS();
  var idga = getCookie('_ga').match(/\d{2,}.{1}\d{2,}/)[0];

  console.log(globoId, iddfp, idga);

</script>

    <a id="main-content"></a>
            		<h1 class="title" id="page-title">Worlds 2014 by the numbers</h1>
                        <div class="block block-system block-main block-system-main odd block-without-title" id="block-system-main">
  <div class="block-inner clearfix">
                
    <div class="content clearfix">
      


<article about="/articles/20141201/1628/worlds-2014-numbers" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" class="node node-article node-published node-not-promoted node-not-sticky author-tsigmund odd clearfix" id="node-article-1628">
        <span property="dc:title" content="Worlds 2014 by the numbers" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>	  
    
    <div class="post-date">Posted on 12-01-14</div>		
		<div class="share-bar">
			<a class="print_ico" href="/print/articles/20141201/1628/worlds-2014-numbers">Print</a>
			<!-- <a class="pdf_ico" href="/printpdf/articles/20141201/1628/worlds-2014-numbers">PDF</a> -->
			<span class='st_email_custom st_ico' displayText='Email'></span>
			<span class='st_twitter_custom st_ico' displayText='Tweet'></span>
			<span class='st_facebook_custom st_ico' displayText='Facebook'></span>
			<span class='st_linkedin_custom st_ico' displayText='LinkedIn'></span>
			<span class='st_google_custom st_ico' displayText='Google'></span>
			<script type="text/javascript">var switchTo5x=true;</script>
			<script type="text/javascript" src="http://w.sharethis.com/button/buttons.js"></script>
			<script type="text/javascript">
				stLight.options({
		        publisher: 'f65a6e51-8a93-4acd-a665-976809c16a17',
		        onhover: false
		    });</script>
		</div>

    
  
  <div class="content clearfix">
    <div class="field field-name-field-main-image field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="http://www.riotgames.com/sites/default/files/styles/article_image/public/content/article/images/main/header_image.png?itok=q9oJg10d" width="700" height="300" alt="Sangham stadium" /></div></div></div><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"> <p dir="ltr"><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">We </span><a href="http://www.riotgames.com/articles/20141027/1568/thanks-sharing-worlds-us" target="_blank">promised we&rsquo;d share viewership numbers</a> once we tallied them up, and the results are in.</p>
<p dir="ltr"><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">Fans around the the world joined us for 15 days of competition, all adding up to over 100 hours of live content broadcast in 19 languages via 40 broadcast partners.</span></p>
<p dir="ltr"><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">In total, across all stages from Taipei to Seoul, we saw </span><strong>288 million cumulative daily unique impressions</strong>. This is a familiar metric that&rsquo;s calculated by taking the unique viewers every day and adding those numbers (but as most fans watched more than one day of the competition, it counts every day they tune in). This adds up to over <strong>179 million hours of esports</strong> watched live online across the world. To put this in perspective, fans watched an overall total of 70 million hours online of the Season 3 World Championship. This year, more fans around the world participated in every step of the journey.</p>
<p dir="ltr"><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">During the final showdown between Samsung White and Royal Club, the peak concurrent viewers (the highest number of fans watching at once) was </span><strong>11.2 million</strong> - a climb from 8.7 million in 2013. Overall total unique viewer count for the finals came in at <strong>27 million</strong>, from 32 million in 2013. During the Finals, fans tuned in for an average online viewtime of <strong>67 minutes</strong>, which beat 2013&rsquo;s average of 42 minutes.</p>
<p dir="ltr"><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">It&rsquo;s awesome to see fans enjoying Worlds as a community, whether it&rsquo;s with 40,000 friends cheering together in Sangam Stadium, or as a group staying up late at a local viewing party halfway across the world. We&rsquo;re honored by your passion and participation. Thank you for tuning in.</span></p>
<p dir="ltr"><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">Next up? We&rsquo;ll unveil some of our plans for 2015 in the coming weeks, so watch this space. Meanwhile, stay tuned to the Expansion Tournament on <a href="http://www.lolesports.com" target="_blank">lolesports.com</a> to see who&rsquo;ll emerge victorious as the newest competitors in the LCS for the 2015 season.</span></p>
<p><span id="docs-internal-guid-3fc7266a-071e-580b-4b36-ac3928259108">Thanks for all the support, and see you for another year of battle in 2015!</span></p>
 </div></div></div>
        
    <span class="print-link"></span><div class="field-group-format group_tags field-group-div group-tags clearfix speed-none effect-none"><h3><span>Tags:</span></h3><div class="field field-name-field-topic field-type-taxonomy-term-reference field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><a href="/topic/esports" typeof="skos:Concept" property="rdfs:label skos:prefLabel">eSports</a></div></div></div></div>  </div>
